nbclient.exceptions.CellExecutionError: An error occurred while executing the following cell:
------------------
import os
from pathlib import Path
from pdf2image import convert_from_path

pdf_dir = r"C:\Users\alamr\OneDrive\Desktop\Checkdat_main\Checkdat_Stampel_AI\1_NyaRitningar"
poppler_path = r"C:\Program Files\poppler-24.08.0\Library\bin"
out_dir = r"C:\Users\alamr\OneDrive\Desktop\Checkdat_main\Checkdat_Stampel_AI\2_output_images"

dpi = 300
fmt = "png"

# Ensure output directory exists
Path(out_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Find all PDFs
pdf_paths = [p for p in Path(pdf_dir).glob("**/*") if p.suffix.lower() == ".pdf"]

print(f"Found {len(pdf_paths)} PDFs")

for pdf in pdf_paths:
    pdf_name = pdf.stem
    print(f"Converting: {pdf}")

    try:
        pages = convert_from_path(
            str(pdf),
            dpi=dpi,
            fmt=fmt,
            poppler_path=poppler_path
        )

        for i, page in enumerate(pages, start=1):
            # Include PDF name in filename to avoid collisions
            out_path = Path(out_dir) / f"{pdf_name}_p{i:03d}.{fmt}"
            page.save(out_path, fmt.upper())

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"!! Failed on {pdf}: {e}")

print("Done.")
